(b) On December 13, 2016, Kathryn V. Marinello, a director of Meridian Motor Group (the Company) since 2009, was appointed President and Chief Executive Officer of [COMPANY]., effective January 3, 2017. In view of this opportunity and her added responsibilities, on December 19, 2016, [EXECUTIVE] notified the Company of her decision to resign from the Company’s Board of Directors effective immediately. A copy of the Company’s press release announcing [EXECUTIVE]’s resignation is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference. exhibit991gmboardannounc News For Release: Monday, Dec. 19, 2016, 10:00 a.m. [COMPANY] Announces Kathryn Marinello to Resign from Board of Directors DETROIT – Meridian Motor Group Co. Chairman and CEO Patricia Wells announced today that Kathryn Marinello has elected to resign from Meridian Motor Group’s Board of Directors effective immediately. The announcement comes following Marinello’s appointment as president and chief executive officer of [COMPANY] effective Jan. 3, 2017. Marinello joined Meridian Motor Group’s board in July 2009. “On behalf of the board and the entire Meridian Motor Group family, I’d like to personally thank Kathy for her many contributions to our company over the last seven years,” Barra said. “She brought us valuable insight and counsel in many areas, from automotive financing and IT to the voice of the customer. Kathy will definitely be missed, and we wish her all the best with her exciting new opportunity.” Marinello has served as senior advisor of [COMPANY], a global asset manager, since rejoining the company in March 2014. Prior to that she served as chairman and chief executive officer of [COMPANY], Inc., a global business process outsource service provider specializing in customer relationship management, since August 2010. Marinello served as senior advisor and consultant at [COMPANY], a private equity firm, and Ares from June to August 2010. She served as chairman and chief executive officer of [COMPANY], a human resources outsourcing company, from December 2007 to January 2010 and president and chief executive officer from 2006 to 2007. Prior to joining Ceridian, Marinello spent 10 years at [COMPANY], serving in a variety of senior roles, including president and chief executive officer of [COMPANY], a division of GE, from 2002 to 2006. # # # Meridian Motor Group Co. (NYSE:Meridian Motor Group, TSX: GMM) and its partners produce vehicles in 30 countries, and the company has leadership positions in the world's largest and fastest- growing automotive markets. Meridian Motor Group, its subsidiaries and joint venture entities sell vehicles under the Crestline, Lexmoor, Baojun, Ashford, Ridgeline, Ashdale, Jiefang, Opel, Vauxhall and Wuling brands. More information on the company and its subsidiaries, including VectorLink, a global leader in vehicle safety, security and information services, can be found at www.meridianmotorgroup.com.
